font-size: x-small;\"><span style=\"font-family: Arial, sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></i></div></div></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 24px;\"><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><div style=\"margin: 0px;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; Something done to one of them will affect the others, coherence establishes communication,&nbsp; some sort of collective vibration was responsible for getting proteins to cooperate with each other and carry out instructions of DNA and cellular proteins.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">  </span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\">Once energy reaches a certain threshold, molecules begin to vibrate in unison, until they reach a level of coherence. The moment molecules reach this state of coherence , they take on certain qualities of of quantum mechanics incl non locality. They get to the point where they can operate in tandem.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black; font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 18.0pt; margin-bottom: .0001pt; margin-bottom: 0in;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Each molecule in the universe had a unique frequency and the language it used to speak to the world was a resonating wave. Molecules speak to each other in oscillating frequencies. The ZPF creates a medium enabling the molecules to speak to each other non locally and virtually instantaneously.</span></span> </span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\" style=\"font-size: 12pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"></span></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\">Electrons glide easily along light pipes without getting entangles in their environment, or settling into any set single state. This means they can remain in quantum state, a condition of all possible states, enabling the brain eventually to finally choose among them. This is free will. At every moment our brains are making quantum choices, taking potential states and making them actual ones.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\"></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\">Newton's classical physics has set mankind back by many decades. In ignoring the effect of ZPF they had eliminated the possibility of interconnectedness and obscured a scientific explanation for many kinds of miracles.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\"></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><span lang=\"EN-GB\">An electron is not a precise entity, but exists as a potential.\u2014a superimposition or sum of all possibilities until we observe or measure it at which point the electron freezes into a particular state. Once we are through looking or measuring the electron dissolves back into the ether of all possibilities. One of the fundamental laws of quantum physics says that an event in the subatomic world exists in all possible states until the act of observing or measuring freezes it or pins it down to a single state. This process is technically known as the collapse of the wave function where wave function means the state of all possibilities.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">  </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"mso-margin-bottom-alt: auto; mso-margin-top-alt: auto;\">\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2017/12/blockchain-bitcoin-big-brother-will.html?showComment=1513185259860#c4671100578196233665\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">December 13, 2017 at 10:44 PM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_175MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nPhysicists in China and the US have built a 10-qubit superconducting quantum processor that could be scaled up to tackle problems not solvable by classical computers.<br />\n<br />\nQubits are the building blocks of quantum computing, capable of superposition \u2013 being in two states at the same time, rather than the computer bits of today, which are either a 1 or a 0 at any given moment.<br />\n<br />\nEntanglement is where quantum states can't be described independently, but only in relation to the others, making for a more solid system. The team used a measurement technique called quantum tomography to prove that they had indeed entangled their qubits<br />\n<br />\nThe phenomenon of entanglement in quantum physics, which has been observed in many experiments, implies that objects that are far removed in space (even across billions of miles) remain connected even though there is no mediating agency.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/01/quantum-entanglement-video-capt-ajit.html</span><br />\n<br />\nVedic philosophy tells us about the existence of another type of particle called the atma, the soul, the self, having different properties from those of ordinary particles.This is not unusual in physics, as is the case with antimatter particles.<br />\n<br />\nThe atma does not come into or out of existence, it is always present. It does not decay or degrade, it maintains its individuality always, it\u2019s infinitesimally small and it\u2019s not composed of more elementary particles. It\u2019s unchangeable, which along with the individuality property implies that it does not unite with other particles to create more complex structures, nor does it merge with others.<br />\n<br />\nThe atma does not interact directly with matter, but given that the atma is the source of consciousness and the life force in a living entity, any entity displaying them reveals the presence of an atma in it\u2014whether human, animal, plant, etc.<br />\n<br />\nVedanta wrote 7000 years ago-- The living entities are not made up of atmas; rather, they are these particles and are animating the material bodies that encase them. As soon as the atma leaves one body for another, the old body no longer exhibits consciousness or life symptoms, and begins to degrade.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/02/daltons-atomic-theory-sage-kashyapa-and.html</span><br />\n<br />\nMaharishi Kashyapa is also known as Kanada Muni. He called the atom Anu. He wrote that there are 108 such elements ...<br />\n<br />\nThe basic Vaisheshika concepts of matter, action, attribute, time and space are described. The 8500 year old Nyaya-Vaiseshika Sutra of Kanada Muni consists of 373 Sutras and is composed of 12 chapters.<br />\n<br />\nIt\u2019s main postulates are:--<br />\n<br />\nAll of the universe is composed of the 5 mahabhuttas and the 4 non physicals: that is Fluid, Atomic elements, fields/force, energy, ether and space, time, mind and soul.<br />\n<br />\nExcept ether, all of the physical elements are made of discreet and distinct paramanus or atoms<br />\n<br />\nSpace-time is a frame in which the physical universe exists<br />\n<br />\nThere are seven categories of experience, which are substance, quality, activity, generality, particularity, inherence, and nonexistence.<br />\n<br />\nEnergy and mass are equivalent.<br />\n<br />\nHere are some of the Sutras: ---<br />\n<br />\nForce is that which displaces, holds together or moves things apart.V.S 1.1.20<br />\nIn the absence of a force, a particle of matter experiences no change. V.S 1.1.6<br />\nThe forces to be considered are an external force, gravity, that with causes attraction of particles, that which causes repulsion of particles and the internal movements of them in matter.<br />\n<br />\nV.S 1.1.13 Action is opposed by an equivalent opposite reaction<br />\nV.S 5.1.1618 The diversities of the movement of an arrow are due to the consecutive changes in the components of the acting forces. The stored energy provides the propulsion to the arrow and this causes it move further to a high point. This component keeps reducing while that of gravity increases resulting in its fall.Once the work against gravity ceases then the body reaches an energyless state falling under gravity.<br />\nV.S 1.1.27 The force on a body is the resultant of gravity and the work done against it.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 2-</div>\n</div>\n<span style=\"color: black;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; Despite of being made of atoms and occupying space air fails show orderly movement so its form cannot be perceived<br />\nV.S 4.1.8 Solids occupy space and assume form due to conglomeration of the constituent particles.<br />\nV.S 4.1.6 The (fluid\u2019s) particles possess energy. The heated particles of air impact the vapor and with this energy it mixes with it. Freezing and melting of a liquid as being a result of heat being taken up or given up by its particles.<br />\nV.S 5.2.9 Some apparently solid substances like ghee, lac and wax are in reality liquids, as their particles are naturally \u201cheat-conjoined\u201d or disorganized as in water. Other true solid substances such as tin, lead, iron, silver and gold need their atoms to be supplied with external heat to disorder them before they become a fluid.<br />\nV.S 2.1.67 Any body\u2019s mass needs to be wholly explained in terms of its constituent particles.<br />\nV.S 1.1.89 A substance can only emerge from another substance and not on its own eventhough its properties change from one to another.<br />\nV.S 9.1.9 Any fundamental particular entity can be a constituent multiple substances.<br />\nV.S 1.1.22 Any substance comprising of two or more primary particle types requires a chemical reaction to generate the conjoining and break up of preexisting molecules.<br />\nV.S 1.1.23 The \u201cmolecules\u201d are stated as emerging from combinations between the fundamental entities.<br />\nV.S 1.1.25 Forces are necessary to bring about combination and break up of molecules.<br />\nV.S 1.1.28 The combinations of particles to produce molecules result in substances with states very different from those of the original particles.<br />\n<br />\nKanada Muni\u2019s laws:<br />\n<br />\nIn the production or increment of karma (i.e. motion), the root cause is force. In other words, there is incremental or decremental change in motion.<br />\nThis law is a law of the measure of force. According to this, so long mechanical force works, there is change in motion i.e. there is momentum. To find its value, it is calculated how much work it produces in a unit time.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 3</div>\n<span class=\"comment-actions secondary-text\" id=\"bc_0_173MN\" kind=\"m\"><span class=\"item-control blog-admin pid-1783552029\" style=\"display: inline;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_173BR\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replybox-single\" id=\"bc_0_173B_box\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; margin-top: 5px;\">\n</div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_174B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c466643263114631994\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_174M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_174MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nCONTINUED FROM 2--<br />\n<br />\nMathematically, the rate of change in momentum i.e. the increment in work in unit time is proportional to the force in action. Also, this change is in the direction of the force. Suppose that the mass of an object is \u2018m\u2019 and in time interval \u2018t\u2019, the velocity of the object changes from \u2018u\u2019 to \u2018v\u2019 due to the force acting on it.<br />\n<br />\nThen, Initial momentum = m*u<br />\nFinal momentum = m*v<br />\nChange in momentum = m(v*u)<br />\nTherefore, the rate of change of momentum = m(v*u)/t<br />\nt = m*a (from Kanada\u2019s first law)<br />\n<br />\nFrom Kandas second law, force is proportional to the rate of change of momentum<br />\nOr, p = k*m*a (where k is a constant)<br />\nIf m=1 and a=1, then<br />\n1 = k*1*1 or k = 1<br />\nOr, p = m*a<br />\n<br />\nTherefore, unit force is the one that produces unit acceleration in an object of unit mass. The VS then goes to say that force is a result of work and is not a physical quantity which is superior to Newtons law that measures it as a physical quantity.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/01/isaac-newton-calculus-thief-capt-ajit.html</span><br />\n<br />\nThe sutras on energy:<br />\n<br />\nVaiseshika defines energy as being a radiant thing(i.e. energy is radiation) and energy is related totemperature and motion of a particle.<br />\n<br />\nVedic Indians understood the process of refraction and absorbtion of energy by \u201cmaterial obstructions\u201d and they understood heat, electricity and magnetism to be forms of energy. It is already understood by the elemental theory that light is also an energy and is composed of discreet units.<br />\n<br />\nThis was of course was not understood in modern times till Max Plank and Einstein in the 20th cetury devised quantum theory after the study of black body radiation and the photoelectric effect.<br />\n<br />\nCapt ajit vadakayil<br />\n..</div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</span></ol>\n<span id=\"bc_0_175b+seedBBVAD\" kind=\"d\">\n</span></div>\n</div>\n</div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 24px; margin-bottom: 0px; margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px; margin-top: 0px;\">\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c8984368294814858237\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot;, times, freeserif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_9M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">Capt. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2017/12/comments-overflow-for-inoperative-load_30.html?showComment=1514595161341#c2849351715198825203\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">December 30, 2017 at 6:22 AM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_7MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nCONTINUED FROM 2-<br />\n<br />\nEntanglement involves putting objects in the peculiar limbo of quantum superposition, in which an object's quantum properties occupy multiple states at once<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/02/schrodinger-father-of-quantum-physics.html</span><br />\n<br />\nPhysicists have entangled particles such as electrons and photons, as well as larger objects such as superconducting electric circuits.<br />\n<br />\nTheoretically, even if entangled objects are separated, their precarious quantum states should remain linked until one of them is measured or disturbed. That measurement instantly determines the state of the other object, no matter how far away. The idea is so counterintuitive that IDIOT Albert Einstein mocked it as \"spooky action at a distance.\"<br />\n<br />\nIn 2015, the most sophisticated of these tests, which involved measuring entangled electrons 1.3 kilometers apart, showed once again that spooky action is real.<br />\n<br />\nBeyond the fundamental result, such experiments also point to the possibility of hack-proof communications.<br />\n<br />\nLong strings of entangled photons, shared between distant locations, can be \"quantum keys\" that secure communications. Anyone trying to eavesdrop on a quantum-encrypted message would disrupt the shared key, alerting everyone to a compromised channel.<br />\n<br />\nPSSSSTTT-- BEFORE CHINA INVENTS THE QUANTUM SATELLITE--WE MUST BREAK THE NATION INTO 4 PARTS AND HAVE TIBET AS A NEIGHBOUR<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nEntangled photons degrade rapidly as they pass through the air or optical fibers. So far, the farthest anyone has sent a quantum key is a few hundred kilometers.<br />\n<br />\nOnce you have satellites distributing your quantum signals throughout the globe, you've done it,--You've leapfrogged all the problems you have with losses in fibers.<br />\n<br />\nJian-Wei Pan, a physicist at the University of Science and Technology of China in Shanghai, got the chance to test the idea when the Micius satellite, was launched in August 2016. The satellite is the foundation of the $100 million Quantum Experiments at Space Scale program<br />\n<br />\nBell's theorem is a \"no-go theorem\" that draws an important distinction between quantum mechanics (QM) and the world as described by classical mechanics<br />\n<br />\nIn its simplest form, Bell's theorem states: No physical theory of local hidden variables can ever reproduce all of the predictions of quantum mechanics.<br />\n<br />\nBell's theorem is the most profound discovery of science.and it is lifted straight out of the Vedas<br />\n<br />\nThere is no need for a faster-than-light signal to tell particle A what measurement has been carried out on particle B, because the universe, including particle A, already 'knows' what that measurement, and its outcome, will be.<br />\n<br />\nLOT OF MY DETRACTORS WERE GUFFAWING LIKE DONKEY WHO HAVE SEEN FRESH SHIT WHEN THEY HEARD THAT MY WIFE MATCHED MORE THAN 500 HOROSCOPES FOR MY ELDER SONs BRIDE<br />\n<br />\nBell\u2019s theorem and subsequent experiments proved the so called entanglements to be right. In such cases, two or more atoms, electrons or photons demonstrate correlated properties even at distances where no communication is possible between them during the given time.<br />\n<br />\nThese developments are the most important developments in the history of physics and the whole of science. They agree with Vedanta. They give rise to the idea of the interconnected wholeness of the world and non-local interactions in contrast to the separate identities with local interactions.<br />\n<br />\nIn their first experiment, the Chinese team sent a laser beam into a light-altering crystal on the satellite. The crystal emitted pairs of photons entangled so that their polarization states would be opposite when one was measured.<br />\n<br />\nThe pairs were split, with photons sent to separate receiving stations in Delingha and Lijiang, 1200 kilometers apart. Both stations are in the mountains of Tibet, reducing the amount of air the fragile photons had to traverse., the team reports simultaneously measuring more than 1000 photon pairs.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nCONTINUED TO 4--</div>\n<span class=\"comment-actions secondary-text\" id=\"bc_0_7MN\" kind=\"m\"><span class=\"item-control blog-admin pid-1783552029\" style=\"display: inline;\"><br /></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-replies\" id=\"bc_0_7BR\" style=\"margin-left: 36px; margin-top: 1em;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-replybox-single\" id=\"bc_0_7B_box\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; margin-top: 5px;\">\n</div>\n</li>\n<li class=\"comment\" id=\"bc_0_8B\" kind=\"b\" style=\"border-bottom: 0px; margin: 0px 0px 16px; padding: 0.25em 0px 0px;\"><div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c5265314992318285551\" style=\"margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_8M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888;\">Capt. (Micius operates only at night.)<br />\n<br />\nIn the next 5 years we plan to launch some really practical quantum satellites, Pan baby says \u2013and I believe him<br />\n<br />\nIn the meantime, Pan baby plans to use Micius to distribute quantum keys to Chinese ground stations, which will require longer strings of photons and additional steps.<br />\n<br />\nThen he wants to demonstrate intercontinental quantum key distribution between stations in China and Austria, which will require holding one half of an entangled photon pair on board until the Austrian ground station appears within view of the satellite.<br />\nPan baby also plans to teleport a quantum state\u2014a technique for transferring quantum-encoded information without moving an actual object\u2014from a third Tibetan observatory to the satellite.<br />\n<br />\nMY ELDER SONs CODING PARTNER IS A CHINK--HE SAYS IS VERY INTELLIGENT<br />\n<br />\nEuropean and U.S. teams are also proposing putting quantum instruments on the International Space Station. One goal is to test whether entanglement is affected by a changing gravitational field, by comparing a photon that stays in the weaker gravitational environment of orbit with an entangled partner sent to Earth.<br />\n<br />\nThere are not many experiments which test links between gravity and quantum physics.<br />\n<br />\nThe implications go beyond record-setting demonstrations: A network of satellites will soon connect the quantum computers being designed in labs worldwide.<br />\n<br />\nAgain --quantum entanglement, one of the odder aspects of quantum theory, links the properties of particles even when they are separated by large distances. When a property of one of a pair of entangled particles is measured, the other \"immediately\" settles down into a state compatible with that measurement.<br />\n<br />\nSo how fast is \"immediately\"?<br />\n<br />\nAccording to research by Prof. Juan Yin and colleagues at the University of Science and Technology of China in Shanghai, the lower limit to the speed associated with entanglement dynamics \u2013 or \"spooky action at a distance\" \u2013 is at least 10,000 times faster than light.<br />\n<br />\nVedas says INSTANTANEOUSLY<br />\n<br />\nNiels Bohr, one of the prime developers of quantum theory, once said that those who are not shocked when they first encounter quantum theory cannot possibly have understood it. line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\"></span>Nothing is wasted \u2013every part of the plant is used like leaf, flower, <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;</span>bark sap neera , seed, oil etc.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; I have seen the ruins of Greece, Rome, and almost all ruins worth seeing on this planet-all small areas. Hampi ruins are scattered over 25 square kilometers !&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: large;\"><b>It takes more than 10 days to see it all.!&nbsp;</b></span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-size: large;\">Hampi , in Bellary district of Karnataka state , was destroyed in 1565, when in the Battle of Talikota , King Rama Raya was beheaded by the Muslim invaders.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/BT70gpN6uYU/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/BT70gpN6uYU&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/BT70gpN6uYU&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">The Muslim invaders then went around destroying a glorious Vijayanagara civilization. They stole and broke , nay , smashed , &nbsp;almost everything, with special attention to the Hindu temples and idols. Stones were carted away to build nearby buildings.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">After that this beautiful city of 25 square kilometers area was left to rot. Today some tourists take pictures .</span><br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"color: magenta; font-size: large;\"><b>The fires raged for more than six months. Every temple and structure had polished decorated rosewood and teakwood statues and beams. ..</b></span><br />\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\"><br /></span>\nThis city was built around a Shiva Linga ( black meteorite holy stone ) on the banks of the mighty Tungabhadra river, as early as 4500 BC.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiLwzDgngI/AAAAAAAADIA/3P6GAs-nWmA/s1600/images+%252863%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiLwzDgngI/AAAAAAAADIA/3P6GAs-nWmA/s1600/images+%252863%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThis was a Dravidian culture.<br />\n<br />\nYou can still see this massive Shiva linga 3 meters high , partly submerged in flowing water inside a temple. text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiDkixZRMI/AAAAAAAADFc/7Mhmhb8TwCQ/s1600/b-hampi-1392.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiDkixZRMI/AAAAAAAADFc/7Mhmhb8TwCQ/s320/b-hampi-1392.jpg\" width=\"318\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nThe monkey king Sugriva's cave is a hot spot for pilgrims. There is something about this natural and ancient cave which draws tourists.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiECzHrqCI/AAAAAAAADFg/ISlv9i4f2Rc/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"239\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiECzHrqCI/AAAAAAAADFg/ISlv9i4f2Rc/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiEVoz7QsI/AAAAAAAADFk/FfonmjPuYT8/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiEVoz7QsI/AAAAAAAADFk/FfonmjPuYT8/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\nNear Sugriva;s cave is Kodandarama temple , where Rama crowned Sugriva as King , after killing his brother Vali.<br />\n<br />\nNext to Sugriva's cave you can find the carved footprints of Rama and his brother Lakhsmana , who fought with Ravana in 4000 BC.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiJui8hWFI/AAAAAAAADGk/EZ_SQ0Bi9ZU/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiJui8hWFI/AAAAAAAADGk/EZ_SQ0Bi9ZU/s1600/images+%25287%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nNearby is the ornate stone chariot, a very endearing image indeed. The stone wheels can turn in the axles.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiHNBl7k6I/AAAAAAAADFw/6_8f2ZvKVCA/s1600/b-hampi-1216.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"480\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiHNBl7k6I/AAAAAAAADFw/6_8f2ZvKVCA/s400/b-hampi-1216.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiHS7zjxMI/AAAAAAAADF0/0_jInAYyivY/s1600/images+%252828%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTiHS7zjxMI/AAAAAAAADF0/0_jInAYyivY/s400/images+%252828%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\nThe chariot faces a dance temple whose pillars are musical , and tourists tap them.<br />\n<br />\nThe Hampi ruins have to be seen to be believed.<br />\n<br />\nThe stones used were local. In Italy and Greece they used white marble. Imagine these Hampi ruins to be milky white like the Taj Mahal or spray painted white . After that the white ruins in Greece and Rome would get an inferiority complex.<br />\n<br />\nProbably the toughness of the stones prevented total obliteration of everything.<br />\n<br />\nEnjoy the pictures of some of the ruins--<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">King Ramaraya of\nAravidu Hindu dynasty ( son-in-law of &nbsp;Vijayanagara emperor Krishna Deva Raya )&nbsp; was killed in the Battle of Talikota on 26\nJanuary 1565), a watershed battle fought between the Vijayanagara Empire and\nthe Muslim Deccan sultanates. &nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; Magnets allow the closing pressure to diminish at a <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">pre-determined system pressure and thereby eliminates pressure <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">accumulation, which is known to cause crew to do manual pressure <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">releases. At the same time, the use of booster systems can be done <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">without or reduced, which actually increases the re-seating pressure, <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">thus, saving VOC or inert gas losses.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">We have used magnets for 30+ years in valves and for the last 7 years in <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">our mag-drive deep-well cargo pumps, too, on chemical carriers including <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">duplex stainless steel tankers. The magnets used are the same in both <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">applications, Neodymium, and they do fine with scalding water for tank <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">cleaning and heated cargo. The magnet force is not lost at these <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">temperatures.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">We also have pure weight-loaded valves in our product range and recently <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">added a pilot operated version, too. We are therefore able to provide <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">basically any performance characteristics wanted, with or without <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">pressure accumulation and with varying re-seating pressures. However, to <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">eliminate stray emissions (leakage), a significant net closing force <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">must be present regardless of the tank pressure, and this is only <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">possible with a controlled valve such as our new pilot operated design. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><br />\n</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Out of the balance of the existing product range, save the pilot <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">operated version, the type you have on board provided the optimum <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">compromise between pressure accumulation and re-seating pressure as well <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">as leakage rates. We are confident you will share our opinion when the <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">hassle with the damaged parts is behind us all.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">For details on the available valve types and our magnet-driven cargo <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">pumps, please refer to www.XXXX.com <http: www.xxx.com=\"\">&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></http:></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Please note that the concept of magnet-driven cargo pumps and the pilot <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">operated valve type is to counteract the very issues you have addressed, <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">in particular crew exposure to cargo and cargo vapour as well as loss of <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">VOC.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Please do not hesitate to contact us if you have any questions or need <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">further information. We would also like to receive any thoughts and <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">comments you may wish to share with us down the line after the pending <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">part replacement. Your comments, bad or good, is a driving momentum for <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">our development.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">Yours truly,<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">XXXX ( Manufatcurer's President)</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\">&nbsp;</span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><o:p>&nbsp;##########################################</o:p></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTeknI41gHI/AAAAAAAADDM/bdC49CRE5a0/s1600/aji.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTeknI41gHI/AAAAAAAADDM/bdC49CRE5a0/s1600/aji.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\"><o:p><br />\n</o:p></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\">CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 YEARS IN COMMAND )</div><div class=\"MsoListParagraph\"><br />\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt.
